// Count occurrences of value v in sequence s
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

// Formalizes the problem statement: a valid assignment of cards to k phone numbers.
// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
// (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and start with 8).
ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

// Necessary and sufficient condition for forming k phone numbers from the cards:

```dafny
// Count occurrences of value v in sequence s
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

// Formalizes the problem statement: a valid assignment of cards to k phone numbers.
// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
// (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and start with 8).
ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

// Necessary and sufficient condition for forming k phone numbers from the cards:
//   - Each phone number requires 11 cards  =>  11 * k <= |digits|
//   - Each phone number requires at least one 8  =>  k <= count of 8s
ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}
```

```dafny
// Count occurrences of value v in sequence s
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

// Formalizes the problem statement: a valid assignment of cards to k phone numbers.
// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
// (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and start with 8).
ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

// Necessary and sufficient condition for forming k phone numbers from the cards:
//   - Each phone number requires 11 cards  =>  11 * k <= |digits|
//   - Each phone number requires at least one 8  =>  k <= count of 8s
ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}
```

--- LLM RESPONSE (575 tokens, 5.76s) ---
<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

// Formalizes the problem statement: a valid assignment of cards to k phone numbers.
// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
// (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and start with 8).
ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

// Necessary and sufficient condition for forming k phone numbers from the cards:
//   - Each phone number requires 11 cards  =>  11 * k <= |digits|
//   - Each phone number requires at least one 8  =>  k <= count of 8s
ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&

//   - Each phone number requires 11 cards  =>  11 * k <= |digits|
//   - Each phone number requires at least one 8  =>  k <= count of 8s
ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)

}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
    invariant 0 <= cnt8 <= i
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  // count of 8s in the whole sequence is cnt8
  var total8 := cnt8;

  // The maximum number of phone numbers that can be formed 
  // is limited by the number of 8s and the total number of cards.
  var maxBy8 := total8;
  var maxByCards := n / 11;

  // The true maximum number of phone numbers is the minimum of these two bounds.
  var best := if maxBy8 < maxByCards then maxBy8 else maxByCards;

  // We also need to ensure that best is achievable, i.e., 11*best <= n.
  // By construction best <= maxByCards = n / 11, hence 11*best <= n.
  // And best <= maxBy8, hence best <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8).
  // Therefore Achievable(best, digits) holds.
  count := best;

  // Verify the postconditions
  assert 11 * count <= n;
  assert count <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8);
  assert count >= 0;

  // Ensure that count + 1 is not achievable
  assert !(11 * (count + 1) <= n && (count + 1) <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8));
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |digits|
    invariant 0 <= cnt8 <= i
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
    decreases |digits| - i
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
    invariant 0 <= i <= |digits|
  {
    if i < |digits| {
      if digits[i] == 8 {
        cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
      }
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }

  assert Achievable(count, digits);
  assert !Achievable(count + 1, digits);
}

ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
    invariant 0 <= cnt8 <= i
  {
    if i < |digits| && digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  assert cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits, 8);

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);

  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }

  assert Achievable(count, digits);
  assert !Achievable(count + 1, digits);
}

// Count occurrences of value v in sequence s
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

// Formalizes the problem statement: a valid assignment of cards to k phone numbers.
// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
// (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and start with 8).
ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

// Necessary and sufficient condition for forming k phone numbers from the cards:
//   - Each phone number requires 11 cards  =>  11 * k <= |digits|
//   - Each phone number requires at least one 8  =>  k <= count of 8s
ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

// Formalizes the problem statement: a valid assignment of cards to k phone numbers.
// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
// (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and start with 8).
ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

// Necessary and sufficient condition for forming k phone numbers from the cards:
//   - Each phone number requires 11 cards  =>  11 * k <= |digits|
//   - Each phone number requires at least one 8  =>  k <= count of 8s
ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
    invariant 0 <= cnt8 <= |digits|
  {

    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
  assert Achievable(count, digits);
  assert !Achievable(count + 1, digits);
}

ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
    invariant 0 <= cnt8 <= |digits|
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
  assert Achievable(count, digits);
  assert !Achievable(count + 1, digits);
}

// Count occurrences of value v in sequence s
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{

}

// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.

--- LLM RESPONSE (434 tokens, 3.1s) ---
<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
    invariant 0 <= cnt8 <= |digits|
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
  assert Achievable(count, digits);
  assert !Achievable(count + 1, digits);
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    assert cnt8 <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8);
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    assert n / 11 <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8);
    count := n / 11;
  }
}
